## Instruction

I'm an accountant in the R&D department of a tech company, and I need your help to organize our department's commuting expense reimbursement forms. Only consider the reimbursement data that comes from taxi bill PDFs located in the 'bills/' folder for the last three months. Please go through all the PDFs and extract the 'File name (excluding file suffixes)', 'Month'(billing period) and 'amount' from each taxi receipt. Then, use these information to fill the Excel file named 'Bill_Format.xlsx'. After filling, change the file name to 'department_expenses.xlsx' and the data processing requirements should refer to 'requirement.txt'.

```python 
import os
import re
from datetime import datetime

# Get list of all PDF files in the bills directory
bills_dir = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/bills"
pdf_files = [f for f in os.listdir(bills_dir) if f.endswith('.pdf') and f.startswith('receipt_')]
pdf_files.sort()

print(f"Found {len(pdf_files)} PDF files to process:")
for f in pdf_files:
    print(f"  {f}")
```

```python 
import subprocess
import json
from collections import defaultdict

# Function to read PDF content using the pdf-tools
def read_pdf_content(pdf_path):
    try:
        # Since we can't directly call the function, we'll store the path for later processing
        return pdf_path
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error reading {pdf_path}: {e}")
        return None

# Store all PDF paths for processing
pdf_paths = []
bills_dir = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/bills"
for filename in pdf_files:
    pdf_path = os.path.join(bills_dir, filename)
    pdf_paths.append((filename, pdf_path))

print(f"Prepared {len(pdf_paths)} files for processing")
print("First 5 files:")
for i, (filename, path) in enumerate(pdf_paths[:5]):
    print(f"  {i+1}. {filename}")
```

```python 
import os
import re
from datetime import datetime
from collections import defaultdict

# Get list of all PDF files in the bills directory
bills_dir = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/bills"
pdf_files = [f for f in os.listdir(bills_dir) if f.endswith('.pdf') and f.startswith('receipt_')]
pdf_files.sort()

# Data structure to store extracted information
taxi_receipts = []

print(f"Processing {len(pdf_files)} PDF files...")

# We'll need to process these one by one using the PDF tools
# For now, let's prepare the structure
for filename in pdf_files:
    file_path = os.path.join(bills_dir, filename)
    # Extract filename without extension
    filename_no_ext = filename.replace('.pdf', '')
    print(f"Will process: {filename_no_ext}")

print("\nReady to extract content from PDFs...")
```

```python 
import re
from datetime import datetime

# Function to extract information from PDF content
def extract_taxi_info(content, filename):
    """Extract taxi receipt information from PDF content"""
    if "TAXI RECEIPT" not in content:
        return None  # Skip non-taxi receipts
    
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', content)
    if not amount_match:
        return None
    
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1))
    
    # Extract date
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', content)
    if not date_match:
        return None
    
    date_str = date_match.group(1)
    date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
    month_str = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    
    # Remove .pdf extension from filename
    filename_no_ext = filename.replace('.pdf', '')
    
    return {
        'filename': filename_no_ext,
        'month': month_str,
        'amount': round(amount, 2),
        'date': date_str
    }

# Test the function with the sample we already read
sample_content = """TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250402373209
Date:
2025-04-02
Time:
10:43
Passenger:
Wang, Lei
Car Number:
BJ-E72032
Driver:
Zhang, W.
Amount:
CNY 61.02
Service Provider: DiDi Express
 Verification QR Code
Note: This receipt is valid for business reimbursement"""

test_result = extract_taxi_info(sample_content, "receipt_20250402_1.pdf")
print("Test extraction result:", test_result)
```

```python 
import os
import re
from datetime import datetime
from collections import defaultdict

# List of all PDF files
pdf_files = [
    'receipt_20250402_1.pdf', 'receipt_20250405_2.pdf', 'receipt_20250407_5.pdf',
    'receipt_20250410_2.pdf', 'receipt_20250411_1.pdf', 'receipt_20250413_1.pdf',
    'receipt_20250414_3.pdf', 'receipt_20250416_3.pdf', 'receipt_20250417_4.pdf',
    'receipt_20250418_5.pdf', 'receipt_20250422_4.pdf', 'receipt_20250424_3.pdf',
    'receipt_20250427_2.pdf', 'receipt_20250430_1.pdf', 'receipt_20250501_3.pdf',
    'receipt_20250504_2.pdf', 'receipt_20250505_2.pdf', 'receipt_20250509_2.pdf',
    'receipt_20250511_4.pdf', 'receipt_20250513_4.pdf', 'receipt_20250515_5.pdf',
    'receipt_20250517_1.pdf', 'receipt_20250524_4.pdf', 'receipt_20250525_1.pdf',
    'receipt_20250526_1.pdf', 'receipt_20250527_5.pdf', 'receipt_20250530_3.pdf',
    'receipt_20250603_1.pdf', 'receipt_20250609_5.pdf', 'receipt_20250610_3.pdf',
    'receipt_20250612_3.pdf', 'receipt_20250614_3.pdf', 'receipt_20250615_2.pdf',
    'receipt_20250616_1.pdf', 'receipt_20250617_2.pdf', 'receipt_20250620_4.pdf',
    'receipt_20250622_5.pdf', 'receipt_20250625_3.pdf', 'receipt_20250627_4.pdf',
    'receipt_20250630_5.pdf'
]

# Function to extract information from PDF content
def extract_taxi_info(content, filename):
    """Extract taxi receipt information from PDF content"""
    if "TAXI RECEIPT" not in content:
        return None  # Skip non-taxi receipts
    
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', content)
    if not amount_match:
        return None
    
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1))
    
    # Extract date
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', content)
    if not date_match:
        return None
    
    date_str = date_match.group(1)
    date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
    month_str = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    
    # Remove .pdf extension from filename
    filename_no_ext = filename.replace('.pdf', '')
    
    return {
        'filename': filename_no_ext,
        'month': month_str,
        'amount': round(amount, 2),
        'date': date_str
    }

# Store the taxi receipts we've already processed
taxi_receipts = []

# Add the ones we've already read
known_taxi_contents = [
    ("receipt_20250402_1.pdf", """TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250402373209
Date:
2025-04-02
Amount:
CNY 61.02"""),
    ("receipt_20250407_5.pdf", """TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250407485619
Date:
2025-04-07
Amount:
CNY 44.46"""),
    ("receipt_20250410_2.pdf", """TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250410651649
Date:
2025-04-10
Amount:
CNY 34.03"""),
    ("receipt_20250413_1.pdf", """TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250413481703
Date:
2025-04-13
Amount:
CNY 43.84"""),
    ("receipt_20250414_3.pdf", """TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250414205270
Date:
2025-04-14
Amount:
CNY 123.14"""),
    ("receipt_20250416_3.pdf", """TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250416354825
Date:
2025-04-16
Amount:
CNY 121.71"""),
    ("receipt_20250417_4.pdf", """TAXI RECEIPT
Receipt No: E20250417354249
Date:
2025-04-17
Amount:
CNY 64.07""")
]

# Process the known taxi receipts
for filename, content in known_taxi_contents:
    info = extract_taxi_info(content, filename)
    if info:
        taxi_receipts.append(info)

print(f"Processed {len(taxi_receipts)} taxi receipts so far:")
for receipt in taxi_receipts:
    print(f"  {receipt['filename']}: {receipt['month']} - CNY {receipt['amount']}")

# Now we need to continue processing the remaining files
remaining_files = [f for f in pdf_files if f not in [item[0] for item in known_taxi_contents]]
print(f"\nRemaining files to process: {len(remaining_files)}")
for f in remaining_files[:10]:  # Show first 10
    print(f"  {f}")
```

```python 
import re
from datetime import datetime
from collections import defaultdict

# Function to extract information from PDF content
def extract_taxi_info(content, filename):
    """Extract taxi receipt information from PDF content"""
    if "TAXI RECEIPT" not in content:
        return None  # Skip non-taxi receipts
    
    # Extract amount using regex
    amount_match = re.search(r'Amount:\s*CNY\s*([\d.]+)', content)
    if not amount_match:
        return None
    
    amount = float(amount_match.group(1))
    
    # Extract date
    date_match = re.search(r'Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})', content)
    if not date_match:
        return None
    
    date_str = date_match.group(1)
    date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
    month_str = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    
    # Remove .pdf extension from filename
    filename_no_ext = filename.replace('.pdf', '')
    
    return {
        'filename': filename_no_ext,
        'month': month_str,
        'amount': round(amount, 2),
        'date': date_str
    }

# All taxi receipt data based on the PDFs we processed
taxi_data = [
    ("receipt_20250402_1.pdf", "2025-04-02", 61.02),
    ("receipt_20250407_5.pdf", "2025-04-07", 44.46),
    ("receipt_20250410_2.pdf", "2025-04-10", 34.03),
    ("receipt_20250413_1.pdf", "2025-04-13", 43.84),
    ("receipt_20250414_3.pdf", "2025-04-14", 123.14),
    ("receipt_20250416_3.pdf", "2025-04-16", 121.71),
    ("receipt_20250417_4.pdf", "2025-04-17", 64.07),
    ("receipt_20250418_5.pdf", "2025-04-18", 51.82),
    ("receipt_20250422_4.pdf", "2025-04-22", 86.43),
    ("receipt_20250427_2.pdf", "2025-04-27", 53.55),
    ("receipt_20250501_3.pdf", "2025-05-01", 53.72),
    ("receipt_20250505_2.pdf", "2025-05-05", 59.45),
    ("receipt_20250509_2.pdf", "2025-05-09", 97.47),
    ("receipt_20250511_4.pdf", "2025-05-11", 106.69),
    ("receipt_20250515_5.pdf", "2025-05-15", 106.92),
    ("receipt_20250517_1.pdf", "2025-05-17", 24.58),
    ("receipt_20250524_4.pdf", "2025-05-24", 88.19),
    ("receipt_20250525_1.pdf", "2025-05-25", 90.96),
    ("receipt_20250527_5.pdf", "2025-05-27", 97.22),
    ("receipt_20250530_3.pdf", "2025-05-30", 97.10),
    ("receipt_20250603_1.pdf", "2025-06-03", 101.20),
    ("receipt_20250609_5.pdf", "2025-06-09", 100.45),
    ("receipt_20250612_3.pdf", "2025-06-12", 59.50),
    ("receipt_20250614_3.pdf", "2025-06-14", 136.94),
    ("receipt_20250615_2.pdf", "2025-06-15", 118.61),
    ("receipt_20250616_1.pdf", "2025-06-16", 86.71),
    ("receipt_20250617_2.pdf", "2025-06-17", 23.18),
    ("receipt_20250620_4.pdf", "2025-06-20", 116.82),
    ("receipt_20250627_4.pdf", "2025-06-27", 70.85),
    ("receipt_20250630_5.pdf", "2025-06-30", 112.91)
]

# Process the taxi receipts
taxi_receipts = []
monthly_totals = defaultdict(float)

for filename, date_str, amount in taxi_data:
    date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
    month_str = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    filename_no_ext = filename.replace('.pdf', '')
    
    receipt = {
        'filename': filename_no_ext,
        'month': month_str,
        'amount': round(amount, 2),
        'date': date_str
    }
    
    taxi_receipts.append(receipt)
    monthly_totals[month_str] += amount

# Sort by date
taxi_receipts.sort(key=lambda x: x['date'])

# Calculate monthly totals
print("TAXI RECEIPTS SUMMARY")
print("====================")
print(f"Total taxi receipts found: {len(taxi_receipts)}")
print()

print("Monthly breakdown:")
for month in sorted(monthly_totals.keys()):
    print(f"{month}: CNY {monthly_totals[month]:.2f}")

total_amount = sum(monthly_totals.values())
print(f"\nTotal amount: CNY {total_amount:.2f}")

print("\nAll taxi receipts:")
for receipt in taxi_receipts:
    print(f"{receipt['filename']}: {receipt['month']} - CNY {receipt['amount']}")
```

```python 
from datetime import datetime
from collections import defaultdict

# All taxi receipt data based on the PDFs we processed
taxi_data = [
    ("receipt_20250402_1.pdf", "2025-04-02", 61.02),
    ("receipt_20250407_5.pdf", "2025-04-07", 44.46),
    ("receipt_20250410_2.pdf", "2025-04-10", 34.03),
    ("receipt_20250413_1.pdf", "2025-04-13", 43.84),
    ("receipt_20250414_3.pdf", "2025-04-14", 123.14),
    ("receipt_20250416_3.pdf", "2025-04-16", 121.71),
    ("receipt_20250417_4.pdf", "2025-04-17", 64.07),
    ("receipt_20250418_5.pdf", "2025-04-18", 51.82),
    ("receipt_20250422_4.pdf", "2025-04-22", 86.43),
    ("receipt_20250427_2.pdf", "2025-04-27", 53.55),
    ("receipt_20250501_3.pdf", "2025-05-01", 53.72),
    ("receipt_20250505_2.pdf", "2025-05-05", 59.45),
    ("receipt_20250509_2.pdf", "2025-05-09", 97.47),
    ("receipt_20250511_4.pdf", "2025-05-11", 106.69),
    ("receipt_20250515_5.pdf", "2025-05-15", 106.92),
    ("receipt_20250517_1.pdf", "2025-05-17", 24.58),
    ("receipt_20250524_4.pdf", "2025-05-24", 88.19),
    ("receipt_20250525_1.pdf", "2025-05-25", 90.96),
    ("receipt_20250527_5.pdf", "2025-05-27", 97.22),
    ("receipt_20250530_3.pdf", "2025-05-30", 97.10),
    ("receipt_20250603_1.pdf", "2025-06-03", 101.20),
    ("receipt_20250609_5.pdf", "2025-06-09", 100.45),
    ("receipt_20250612_3.pdf", "2025-06-12", 59.50),
    ("receipt_20250614_3.pdf", "2025-06-14", 136.94),
    ("receipt_20250615_2.pdf", "2025-06-15", 118.61),
    ("receipt_20250616_1.pdf", "2025-06-16", 86.71),
    ("receipt_20250617_2.pdf", "2025-06-17", 23.18),
    ("receipt_20250620_4.pdf", "2025-06-20", 116.82),
    ("receipt_20250627_4.pdf", "2025-06-27", 70.85),
    ("receipt_20250630_5.pdf", "2025-06-30", 112.91)
]

# Process the taxi receipts
taxi_receipts = []
monthly_totals = defaultdict(float)

for filename, date_str, amount in taxi_data:
    date_obj = datetime.strptime(date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
    month_str = date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m')
    filename_no_ext = filename.replace('.pdf', '')
    
    receipt = {
        'filename': filename_no_ext,
        'month': month_str,
        'amount': round(amount, 2),
        'date': date_str
    }
    
    taxi_receipts.append(receipt)
    monthly_totals[month_str] += amount

# Sort by date
taxi_receipts.sort(key=lambda x: x['date'])

# Prepare the data for Excel
taxi_receipts_data = []
for receipt in taxi_receipts:
    taxi_receipts_data.append([receipt['filename'], receipt['month'], receipt['amount']])

# Monthly totals (rounded to 2 decimal places)
april_total = round(monthly_totals['2025-04'], 2)
may_total = round(monthly_totals['2025-05'], 2) 
june_total = round(monthly_totals['2025-06'], 2)
total_amount = round(april_total + may_total + june_total, 2)

print("Data to be filled in Excel:")
print("=========================")
print(f"Department: R&D Department")
print(f"Applicant's name: Lei WANG")
print()
print(f"April 2025 total: {april_total}")
print(f"May 2025 total: {may_total}")
print(f"June 2025 total: {june_total}")
print(f"Total amount: {total_amount}")
print()
print(f"Number of detail records: {len(taxi_receipts_data)}")
print("Sample detail records:")
for i, record in enumerate(taxi_receipts_data[:3]):
    print(f"  {record[0]} | {record[1]} | {record[2]}")
print("...")
```
</div>
